msg:It is very convenient to book a room on Ctrip. This time, I also used Ctrip's money to spend. There is no deposit and any fees for check-in. It is very convenient to deduct the money after leaving the store. The parent-child room booked was originally written on the 6th-7th floor. The front desk gave the family room on the 10th floor. The higher floors have a better view and are farther away from the air-conditioning host below. The room is a 1.8-meter big bed and a 1.2-meter small bed. The bathroom has a shower and a bathtub. There are two washbasins. The toilet and shower are separated by two glass compartments. The breakfast is not very rich, but it is considered to be in line with the standard of this standard hotel. There are freshly cooked noodles, wontons, gnocchi, coffee, milk, orange juice, and fruit supplements are fairly timely. The first day of check-in is a working day, people Relatively few, the waiter also took the initiative to ask if you want coffee or black tea, which is a good one. Before driving out every day, you need to scan a QR code at the front desk. Pay attention to distinguish whether it is on the ground or underground. The code is divided into two. There are quite a few restaurants near the hotel. I walked to the river bank for about 2 kilometers. The first day was the fifteenth day of the ***** calendar, and I saw a big full moon. It's really close to Daqi Mountain, it takes only 5 minutes to drive there.
Some shortcomings: The TV connection in the room was not very good. The waiter adjusted it on the first day, unplugged the cable and plugged it in again. The signal was normal, but the situation continued to occur from time to time in the next few days. I hope the hotel will check it thoroughly. There are not many hotel facilities, there is no swimming pool, only a small gym.
